Location: 5 minutes by taxi to the opposite Shilaoren Beach; 5 minutes walk to the shopping mall; 5 minutes walk to the subway
Breakfast: There is a semi-buffet breakfast on the 51st floor. Compared with the full buffet breakfast on the 3rd floor of MGM, there are fewer people, better service, and more exquisite breakfast.
Room: The facilities are new and the decoration is high-end, and the details are in place!
Service: The room service responds promptly, and the waiters and front desk are very nice.
In addition, I would like to thank our housekeeper Icey. Her service made the stay experience of Diaoyu Island even better. She informed us of the local weather one day in advance and patiently asked about the check-in requirements; she also arranged a corner room for us in advance when she learned that we had two children (not only the room was large, but also the 270-degree view room had a particularly good view); she sent us a self-made travel guide; and she took the initiative to provide us with a late check-out on the last day. During the stay, our questions and needs were basically answered in seconds.
It was a very happy experience. Next time I come to Qingdao, I will choose Diaoyu Island again.

msg:It was my first time to come to Qingdao, and I chose the Qingdao Diaoyutai Hotel, which was newly opened in June 2023, for my first night. The butler-style service and the very considerate check-in care from Chen Xi at the front desk left a very deep impression on me.
    üìçLocation
      The third MGM Diaoyutai Hotel in China did not choose to be located near the densely populated May Fourth Square. Instead, it opened on the T1 floor of No. 195 Hong Kong East Road, Laoshan District, where you can enjoy the Shichangzha Bathing Beach and the wide sea view.
     üå†Lobby
      As the new landmark of Laoshan, the mansion in the sky, the hotel building exterior was designed by the New York office of KPF;
The exterior adopts the design concept of portal (tower) and Chinese-style treasure box tower, which is rising steadily. The hotel design is from the hands of Canadian design master Alessandro Munge. He has managed classic hotels such as the Rosewood in New York and the Park Hyatt in Toronto.
The most eye-catching thing in the lobby are two huge curved screens, which show vivid pictures of Qingdao‚Äôs mountains and seas as the light changes over time.
      üõèÔ∏èRoom
      The hotel has a total of 116 rooms, starting from 45 square meters. The red painted door shows a theme from the azure sea to the royal courtyard, from ocean blue, sunset gold, to Chinese red. Each theme shows noble color charm. The design of the elevator car is inspired by the traditional sedan. The exquisite materials and silk embroidery details fully interpret the Chinese craftsmanship spirit.
  ü•ÇFood:
    There are 5 restaurants including lobby bar, dessert house, all-day dining restaurant Huanyan, Yishuo Restaurant and "Red" Bar.
‚ùáÔ∏èAll-day dining restaurant - Feast: The main tone is blue and white, which connects a scene of seaside islands, and uses fresh ingredients from all over the world.
‚ùáÔ∏èYishuo Restaurant: Full of art, a hand-blown glass art decorative lamp in the center of the restaurant is based on cedar, surrounded by scattered wooden devices.
‚ùáÔ∏è"Red" Bar: Become the best place after dark.

üîπSurrounding attractions: Shichangzhe Beach, Qingdao Museum, Qingdao Polar Ocean Park, etc.
üîπAddress: T1 Floor, No. 195 Hong Kong East Road, Laoshan District, Qingdao, Shandong
üîπHow to get there:
Take a taxi, it‚Äôs about 23 minutes‚Äô drive from Qingdao North Railway Station and about 25 minutes‚Äô drive from Qingdao Station!
Take National Subway Line 2 to Miaoling Road Subway Station - Exit F and walk for about 3 minutes!

üåüTo be honest, there are many remarkable things about this new Diaoyutai Hotel. The overall a**osphere and quiet environment form a very sharp contrast with the modern and flamboyant environment of the MGM Hotel next to it. Provides customers with a variety of choices.
